 krishi laagat or keemat nirdhaaran ayog (CACP) ne 2018-19 ke liye kharif sijan kii 14 badi fasalon ke liye emspi kii gananaa pichley saal ke laagat ke aadhaar par kii he

 This was the demand of farmers
 The government has set a new benchmark for calculating minimum support price by 50% more than A2 + FL, while farmers are demanding C2 + 50% as per the recommendation of Swaminathan Commission
